<script src="https://api-maps.yandex.ru/2.1/?apikey=f9a4c3af-7508-4b35-bcf5-2e1cf8ae0173&lang=en_US" type="text/javascript"></script>



<script>

function openModalMetadata() {
  var modalmeta = document.getElementById("ModalMeta");
  modalmeta.style.display = "block";
}

// Close the modal
function closeModalMetadata() {
  var modalmeta = document.getElementById("ModalMeta");
  modalmeta.style.display = "none";
}

document.addEventListener("click", function(event) {
    var modalmeta = document.getElementById("ModalMeta");
  if (event.target === modalmeta) {
    modalmeta.style.display = "none";
  }
}); 


ymaps.ready(init);
    function init(){ 
        var myMap = new ymaps.Map("map", {
            center: [50.054859023597345, 17.117379179237027],
            zoom: 4,
            controls: []
        });

        myMap.controls.add('zoomControl');

        myMap.events.add('click', function (e) {
            var coords = e.get('coords');
            let xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
            xhr.open("GET", "https://geocode-maps.yandex.ru/1.x?geocode="+coords[1]+","+coords[0]+"&apikey=f9a4c3af-7508-4b35-bcf5-2e1cf8ae0173&format=json&lang=en_Us");
            xhr.onreadystatechange = function () {
            if (xhr.readyState === 4) {
                res = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
                var city = res['response']['GeoObjectCollection']['featureMember'][0]['GeoObject']['metaDataProperty']['GeocoderMetaData']['text'];
                $('#gpsMeta').val(coords[1]+", "+coords[0]);
                $('#sdsdfd').html('');
                $('#sdsdfd').html(coords[1]+", "+coords[0]+" <br> "+city);
                $('#dfsdfsdfsffd').show();
            }};
            xhr.send();                 
        });
    }

    const inputElement324234234 = document.getElementById("gpsMeta");
    inputElement324234234.addEventListener("input", function(event) {
        $('#dfsdfsdfsffd').hide();
    });    

    function randomGPSFn() {
        var long = (Math.random()*360-180).toFixed(8);
        var lat = (Math.random()*180-90).toFixed(8);
        $("#gpsMeta").val(long+", "+lat);
        $('#sdsdfd').html('');
        $('#dfsdfsdfsffd').hide();
    }

    function randomTimeMetaFn() {
        const getRandomNumber = (min, max) => Math.floor(Math.random() * (max - min + 1)) + min;
        const formatNumber = number => number.toString().padStart(2, '0');   
        const hours = getRandomNumber(0, 23);
        const minutes = getRandomNumber(0, 59);
        const seconds = getRandomNumber(0, 59);
        const res = `${formatNumber(hours)}:${formatNumber(minutes)}:${formatNumber(seconds)}`;        
        $('#timeMeta').val(res);
    }

    $("#countryesId").select2();
    $('#countryflag').css('opacity', '1');


    function showToast() {
  const toast = document.getElementById("myToast");
  toast.classList.add("show");
  setTimeout(() => {
    toast.classList.remove("show");
  }, 4000);
}


    jQuery(function($){
	    $(document).mouseup( function(e){
		    var div = $( ".modaledit-content" );
		    var div1 = $( ".dsfsdfdsfsfsdfdsf" );
		    var div2 = $( ".dsfsdfdsfsfsdfdsf1" );
		    if ( !div.is(e.target) && div.has(e.target).length === 0 ) {
                if( $(".modaledit-content").css('display') == 'block') {
                    div.hide(); 
			        $('#modalEdit').hide();
                }
		    }
            if ( !div1.is(e.target) && div1.has(e.target).length === 0 ) {
                if( $(".dsfsdfdsfsfsdfdsf").css('display') == 'block') {
                    div1.hide();
			        $('#modalEditSign').hide();
                }
		    }
            if ( !div2.is(e.target) && div2.has(e.target).length === 0 ) {
                if( $(".dsfsdfdsfsfsdfdsf1").css('display') == 'block') {
                    div2.hide();
			        $('#modalEditSign2').hide(); 
                }
		    }
	    });
    });  

</script>
